   ŚĀ 1,1	ŚĀ 1,1
   prajāpatir vai saṃvatsaraḥ | tasyaiṣa ātmā yan mahāvratam | tasmād enat	prajApatiH vE saMvatsaraH | tasya-ezaH AtmA yat mahA-vratam | tasmAt enat-
   parasmai na śaṃsen net sarveṣāṃ bhūtānām ātmānaṃ parasmin dadhānīti ||	parasmE na SaMset net sarvezAm BUtAnAm AtmAnam parasmin daDAni-iti ||
   atho indrasyaiṣa ātmā yan mahāvratam | tasmād enat parasmai na śaṃsen ned	aTo indrasya-ezaH AtmA yat mahA-vratam | tasmAt enat parasmE na SaMset ned
   indrasyātmānaṃ parasmin dadhānīti || atho yam evaitam ṛṅmayaṃ yajurmayaṃ	indrasya-AtmAnam parasmin daDAni-iti || aTo yam eva-etam Rc-mayam yajuH-mayam
   sāmamayaṃ puruṣaṃ saṃskurvanti tasyaiṣa ātmā yan mahāvratam | tasmād enat	sAma-mayam puruzam saMskurvanti tasya-ezaH AtmA yat mahA-vratam | tasmAt enat-
   parasmai na śaṃsen net sarveṣāṃ chandasām ātmanaṃ parasmin dadhānīti ||	parasmE na SaMset net sarvezAm CandasAm Atmanam parasmin daDAni-iti ||
   kāmaṃ tu sattriṇāṃ hotā śaṃset | pitre vācāryāya vātmane haivāsya	kAmam tu sattriNAm hotA SaMset | pitre vA-AcAryAya vA-Atmane ha-eva-asya
   tacchandastaṃ bhavati | ātmanaiva tad yajñaṃ samardhayati | tasya	tad-CandaH-tam Bavati | AtmanA-eva tat yajQam samarDayati | tasya
   pañcaviśaḥ stomaḥ | caturviṃśatir vai saṃvatsarasyārdhamāsāḥ,	paQca-viSaH stomaH | caturviMSatiH vE saMvatsarasya-arDa-mAsAH,
   saṃvatsarasyaivāptyai | atho prajāpatir vai saṃvatsaraḥ pañcaviṃśaḥ | atho	saMvatsarasya-eva-AptyE | aTo prajApatiH vE saMvatsaraH paQcaviMSaH | aTo
   caturviṃśo vai purastāt kṛto bhavati tasyaiṣa gatir yat pañcaviṃśaḥ |	caturviMSaH vE purastAt kRtaH Bavati tasya-eza gatiH yat paQcaviMSaH |
   aindraśca ṛṣabhaḥ prājāpatyaścāja upālabhyau | aindraṃ vā etad ahaḥ |	EndraH-ca RzaBaH prAjApatyaH-ca-aja upAlaByO | Endram vE etat ahar |
   indra u vai prajāpatiḥ | tat prājāpatyaṃ rūpam | atho etad eva	indraH u vE prajApatiH | tat prAjApatyam rUpam | aTo etat eva
   paśuṣvaindraṃ rūpaṃ yad ṛṣabhaḥ ||	paSuzu-Endram rUpam yat RzaBaH ||
   ŚĀ 1,2	ŚĀ 1,2
   tasya viśoviśo vo atithim iti dvādaśarcam ājyam | dvādaśa vai māsāḥ	tasya viSaH-viSaH vaH atiTim iti dvAdaSa-Rcam Ajyam | dvAdaSa vE mAsAH

   yāvannaraścakṣasā dīdhyānā ityetena rūpeṇa | ud vāṃ cakṣurvaruṇa	yAvat-naraH-cakzasA dIDyAnAH iti-etena rUpeNa | ud vAm cakzuH-varuNa

   rūpeṇa | kathā mahām avṛdhat kasya hotur ityaindraṃ mahadvad vṛdhavat |	rUpeNa | kaTA mahAm avRDat kasya hotuH iti-Endram mahadvat vRDavat |

   vaiśvadevaṃ sahīyaso varuṇa mitra martād ityetena rūpeṇa | uta syā naḥ	vESvadevam sahIyasaH varuNa mitra martAt iti-etena rUpeNa | uta syAH naH
   sarasvatī juṣāṇeti sarasvataṃ dvārāvṛtasya subhago vyāvar ityetena rūpeṇa	sarasvatI juzANa-iti sarasvatam dvAra-AvRtasya suBagaH vyAvar iti-etena rUpeNa
   | eṣa vā u kadvāṃstraiṣṭubhas tṛcakl̥pto vāmadevyaḥ praügaḥ | prajāpatir	| eza vE u kadvAn=-trEzwuBaH tRca-kl̥ptaH vAmadevyaH praügaH | prajApatiH-

   ŚĀ 1,3	ŚĀ 1,3

   ŚĀ 1,4	ŚĀ 1,4

   ŚĀ 1,8	ŚĀ 1,8

   vṛṣṭiṃ varṣati | dyāvāpṛthivyau samadhātām ityadhidaivatam | athādhyātmam	vRzwim varzati | dyAvApRTivyO samaDAtAm iti-aDidEvatam | aTa-aDyAtmam
   | puruṣo 'yaṃ sarvam āṇḍam | dve vidale bhavataḥ | tatredam eva pūrvarūpam	| puruzaH ayam sarvam ANxam | dve vidale BavataH | tatra-idam eva pUrva-rUpam
   idam uttararūpam | tatrāyam antareṇākāśaḥ | yathāsau dyāvāpṛthivyor	idam uttara-rUpam | tatra-ayam antareNa-AkASaH | yaTA-asO dyAvApRTivyoH-
   antareṇākāśa etasminn ākāśe prāṇa āyatto bhavati yathāmuṣminn ākāśe vāyur	antareNa-AkASaH etasmin AkASe prANaH AyattaH Bavati yaTA-amuzmin AkASe vAyuH-
   āyatto bhavati | yathāmūni trīṇi jyotīṃṣyevam imāni puruṣe trīṇi jyotīṃṣi	AyattaH Bavati | yaTA-amUni trINi jyotIMzi-evam imAni puruze trINi jyotIMzi
   | yathāsau divyāditya evam idaṃ śirasi cakṣuḥ | yathāsāvantarikṣe vidyud	| yaTA-asO divya-AdityaH evam idam Sirasi cakzuH | yaTA-asO=-antarikze vidyut-
   evam idam ātmani hṛdayam | yathāyam agniḥ pṛthivyam evam idam upasthe	evam idam Atmani hRdayam | yaTA-ayam agniH pRTivyam evam idam upasTe
   retaḥ | evamiva ha sma sarvata ātmānam anuvidhāyāha - idam eva pūrvarūpam	retaH | evam-iva ha sma sarvatas AtmAnam anuviDAya-Aha  idam eva pUrvarUpam

   saṃhitāṃ +veda saṃdhīyate prajayā paśubhir yaśasā brahmavarcasena svargeṇa	saMhitAm +veda saMDIyate prajayA paSuBiH yaSasA brahmavarcasena svargeNa
   lokena sarvam āyur eti ||	lokena sarvam AyuH eti ||
   ŚĀ 7,5	ŚĀ 7,5

   ŚĀ 7,9	ŚĀ 7,9
   athāto 'nuvyāhārāḥ | prāṇo vaṃśa iti vidyāt | sa ya enaṃ prāṇaṃ vaṃśaṃ	aTa-atas anuvyAhArAH | prANaH vaMSaH iti vidyAt | sa yaH enam prANam vaMSam
   bruvan param upavadet śaknuvan kaścic cen manyeta - prāṇaṃ vaṃśaṃ	bruvan param upavadet Saknuvan kaScid ced manyeta  prANam vaMSam
   +samadhām | prāṇaṃ vaṃśaṃ saṃdhitsituṃ na śaknoṣītyāttha | prāṇas tvā	+samaDAm | prANam vaMSam saMDitsitum na Saknozi-iti-AtTa | prANaH tvA
   vaṃśo hāsyatītyevainaṃ brūyāt | atha ced aśaknuvan manyeta prāṇaṃ vaṃśaṃ	vaMSaH hAsyati-iti-eva-enam brUyAt | aTa ced aSaknuvan manyeta prANam vaMSam
   samadhitsīḥ taṃ nāśakaḥ saṃdhātuṃ prāṇas tvā vaṃśo hāsyatītyevainaṃ brūyāt	samaDitsIH tam na-aSakaH saMDAtum prANaH tvA vaMSaH hAsyati-iti-eva-enam brUyAt-

   ŚĀ 7,10	ŚĀ 7,10
   sa yadi prāṇaṃ vaṃśaṃ bruvantaṃ param upavadet śaknuvantaṃ cen manyeta -	sa yadi prANam vaMSam bruvantam param upavadet Saknuvantam ced manyeta -
   prāṇaṃ vaṃśaṃ samadhitsiṣam prāṇaṃ vaṃśaṃ saṃdhitsituṃ na śaknoṣītyāttha |	prANam vaMSam samaDitsizam prANam vaMSam saMDitsitum na Saknozi-iti-AtTa |

   ŚĀ 7,11	ŚĀ 7,11

   ŚĀ 7,16	ŚĀ 7,16

   nānantevāsine vā brūyād iti | ya imām adbhiḥ parigṛhītāṃ vasumatīṃ	na-anantevAsine vA brUyAt iti | yaH imAm adBiH parigRhItAm vasumatIm
   dhanasya pūrṇāṃ dadyād idam eva tato bhūya idam eva tato bhūya ity	Danasya pUrNAm dadyAt idam eva tatas BUyas idam eva tatas BUyaH iti-
   anuśāsanam | tām etām upaniṣadaṃ vedaśiro na yathā kathaṃ cana vadet | tad	anuSAsanam | tAm etAm upanizadam vedaSiraH na yaTA kaTam cana vadet | tat-
   etad ṛcābhyuditam ||	etat RcA-aByuditam ||
   iti śāṅkhāyanāraṇyake trayodaśamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||	iti SAFKAyana-AraNyake trayodaSamaH aDyAyaH ||
   ŚĀ 14,1	ŚĀ 14,1
   ṛcāṃ mūrdhānaṃ yajuṣām uttamāṅgam | sāmnāṃ śiro 'tharvāṇāṃ muṇḍamuṇḍam |	RcAm mUrDAnam yajuzAm uttamAFgam | sAmnAm SiraH aTarvANAm muNxa-muNxam |
   nādhīte 'dhīte vedam āhus tam ajñam | śiraś chitvāsau kurute kabandham ||	na-aDIte aDIte vedam AhuH tam ajQam | SiraH CitvA-asO kurute kabanDam ||
   ŚĀ 14,2	ŚĀ 14,2
   sthāṇur ayaṃ bhārahāraḥ kilābhūt | adhītya vedaṃ na vijānāti yo 'rtham |	sTANuH ayam BArahAraH kila-aBUt | aDItya vedam na vijAnAti yaH arTam |
   yo 'rthajña it sakalaṃ bhadram aśnute | nākam eti jñānavidhūtapāpmā ||	yaH arTa-jQaH id sakalam Badram aSnute | nAkam eti jQAna-viDUta-pApmA ||

   ŚĀ 15,1	ŚĀ 15,1
   atha vaṃśaḥ | oṃ namo brahmaṇe nama ācāryebhyaḥ | guṇākhyāc chāṅkhāyanād	aTa vaMSaH | om namaH brahmaNe namaH AcAryeByaH | guNa-AKyAt SAFKAyanAt-
   asmābhir adhītam | guṇākhyaś śāṅkhāyanaḥ kahoḷāt kauṣītakeḥ | kahoḷaḥ	asmABiH aDItam | guNa-AKyaH SAFKAyanaH kaho?At kOzItakeH | kaho?aH
   kauṣītakir uddālakād āruṇeḥ | uddālaka āruṇiḥ priyavratāt saumāpeḥ |	kOzItakiH uddAlakAt AruNeH | uddAlakaH AruNiH priyavratAt sOmApeH |
   priyavrataḥ saumāpiḥ somapāt | somapaḥ saumāt prātiveśyāt | saumaḥ	priyavrataH sOmApiH somapAt | somapaH sOmAt prAtiveSyAt | sOmaH
   prātiveśyaḥ prativeśyāt | prativeśyo bṛhaddivāt | bṛhaddivaḥ sumnayoḥ |	prAtiveSyaH prativeSyAt | prativeSyaH bRhat-divAt | bRhaddivaH sumnayoH |
   sumnayur uddālakāt | uddālako viśvamanasaḥ | viśvamanā vyaśvāt | vyaśvaḥ	sumnayuH uddAlakAt | uddAlakaH viSva-manasaH | viSva-manAH vyaSvAt | vyaSvaH
   sākamaśvāt | sākamaśvo devarātāt | devarāto viśvāmitrāt | viśvāmitra	sAkamaSvAt | sAkamaSvaH devarAtAt | devarAtaH viSvAmitrAt | viSvAmitra
   indrāt | indraḥ prajāpateḥ | prajāpatir brahmaṇaḥ | brahmā svayaṃbhūḥ |	indrAt | indraH prajApateH | prajApatiH brahmaNaH | brahmA svayaMBUH |
   namo brahmaṇe namo brahmaṇe ||	namaH brahmaNe namaH brahmaNe ||
